train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 27 @@@ 14 @@@  pasted below 
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 29 @@@ 7 @@@ metrics
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 30 @@@ 80 @@@ spark has a configurable metrics system based on the dropwizard metrics library 
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 31 @@@ 90 @@@ this allows users to report spark metrics to a variety of sinks including http jmx and csv
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 32 @@@ 88 @@@ files the metrics system is configured via a configuration file that spark expects to be
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 33 @@@ 89 @@@ present at spark home conf metrics properties a custom file location can be specified via
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 34 @@@ 46 @@@ the spark metrics conf configuration property 
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 35 @@@ 95 @@@ by default the root namespace used for driver or executor metrics is the value of spark app id 
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 36 @@@ 89 @@@ however often times users want to be able to track the metrics across apps for driver and
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 37 @@@ 67 @@@ executors which is hard to do with application id i e spark app id 
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 38 @@@ 87 @@@ since it changes with every invocation of the app for such use cases a custom namespace
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 39 @@@ 92 @@@ can be specified for metrics reporting using spark metrics namespace configuration property 
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 40 @@@ 88 @@@ if say users wanted to set the metrics namespace to the name of the application they can
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 41 @@@ 72 @@@ set the spark metrics namespace property to a value like spark app name 
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 42 @@@ 91 @@@ this value is then expanded appropriately by spark and is used as the root namespace of the
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 43 @@@ 84 @@@ metrics system non driver and executor metrics are never prefixed with spark app id 
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 44 @@@ 83 @@@ nor does the spark metrics namespace property have any such affect on such metrics 
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 45 @@@ 89 @@@ spark s metrics are decoupled into different instances corresponding to spark components 
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 46 @@@ 87 @@@ within each instance you can configure a set of sinks to which metrics are reported the
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 47 @@@ 44 @@@ following instances are currently supported 
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 48 @@@ 44 @@@  master the spark standalone master process 
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 49 @@@ 82 @@@  applications a component within the master which reports on various applications 
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 50 @@@ 42 @@@  worker a spark standalone worker process 
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 51 @@@ 27 @@@  executor a spark executor 
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 52 @@@ 83 @@@  driver the spark driver process the process in which your sparkcontext is created 
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 53 @@@ 42 @@@  shuffleservice the spark shuffle service 
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 54 @@@ 103 @@@ each instance can report to zero or more sinks sinks are contained in the org apache spark metrics sink
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 55 @@@ 8 @@@ package 
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 56 @@@ 53 @@@  consolesink logs metrics information to the console 
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 57 @@@ 64 @@@  csvsink exports metrics data to csv files at regular intervals 
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 58 @@@ 56 @@@  jmxsink registers metrics for viewing in a jmx console 
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 59 @@@ 81 @@@  metricsservlet adds a servlet within the existing spark ui to serve metrics data
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 60 @@@ 13 @@@ as json data 
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 61 @@@ 47 @@@  graphitesink sends metrics to a graphite node 
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 62 @@@ 49 @@@  slf4jsink sends metrics to slf4j as log entries 
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 63 @@@ 94 @@@ spark also supports a ganglia sink which is not included in the default build due to licensing
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 64 @@@ 13 @@@ restrictions 
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 65 @@@ 64 @@@  gangliasink sends metrics to a ganglia node or multicast group 
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 66 @@@ 86 @@@ to install the gangliasink you ll need to perform a custom build of spark note that by
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 67 @@@ 53 @@@ embedding this library you will include lgpl licensed
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 68 @@@ 88 @@@ code in your spark package for sbt users set the spark ganglia lgpl environment variable
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 69 @@@ 85 @@@ before building for maven users enable the pspark ganglia lgpl profile in addition to
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 70 @@@ 106 @@@ modifying the cluster s spark build user applications will need to link to the spark ganglia lgplartifact 
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 71 @@@ 89 @@@ the syntax of the metrics configuration file is defined in an example configuration file 
train_291.ann @@@ Body @@@ 72 @@@ 45 @@@  spark home conf metrics properties template
